        <span class="nav-featured">Featured Product</span>
        <h2 class="uber-nav-title">Tax calculation</h2>
    </div>
    <div class="clearfix"></div>
        <p>
      Telecommunications taxes have complex rules that can be difficult to understand. Avalara for Communications connects to your current billing or ERP system to quickly and automatically file your taxes.
        </p>

        <h2 class="uber-nav-title">Solutions for Vacation Rentals and Home Shares</h2>
    </div>
